22a1(12): a// rgyal so ru mgrin lag ya/ khyed kyi bka' 'tshin ma bgyid na / ba ga cag rgul du brug sar 'gyur / ces klu rnams gyis ama bcas theng/ rjes sa yi rangs nas mngon/ 
22a2(12): sarg go' / sal chen so ru mgrin ni ces nyid kyi byins pa khrim par gyur tong/ krlu rnams rang gis gnas so es nas ngam tshig la gnas par gyur tog/ lung bstan am bcas/ 
22a3(12): sa'i le'u ste su zu ba na so'o / na ga kru ' la zhes bya ba'i rgyud s+dzobgs so/ shin r'di mtshobbs gb 'las byas no tshing mhas/ tshin lub 'brel bar/ 
22a4(12): bcas cran gyitshong pro ghrib byan na ng tshig li 'pel/ #rpa ni mgyen spyas zobbar /
